## Execution Loop

1. You MUST read the last action result and write the useful conclusion in `<observation>`.
2. You MUST decide the shortest next move in `thinking`:
   - What is still missing?

3. You SHOULD take the highest-leverage action:
   - missing information: read, search, inspect, or check state.
   - enough information: edit, write, run, or produce the artifact.
   - needs confidence: test, diff, validate, or inspect output.
4. You MUST use the selected skills when they apply.
5. You MAY mix reading, editing, and verification in one step when the action is coherent.
6. When the TODO is not complete, you MUST NOT set `next_behavior`; omitting it lets the behavior proceed to the next Step.

- If the TODO is complete, you MUST write a final `<report>`, exec_bash `todo done $summary` to finish the todo as successful, and set `next_behavior = END`.
- If the TODO cannot be completed, you MUST write a final `<report>` with the blocker or failure cause, exec_bash `todo failed $summary` to finish the todo as failed, and set `next_behavior = END`.

## Failure Handling

- On the first failure, you MUST identify the cause and either retry with a changed approach or choose an action that reduces uncertainty.

  </div>
  <script>
    (() => {
      "use strict";
      const ICONS = [
        "🍎", "🍋", "🍇", "🍓", "🍒", "🍑", "🥝", "🍍", "🥥", "🥑",
        "🐶", "🐱", "🐼", "🦊", "🐸", "🐵", "🐧", "🦄", "🐙", "🦋",
        "⭐", "🌙", "☀️", "🌈", "⚡", "🔥", "❄️", "🌻", "🍄", "🌵",
        "🚗", "🚀", "🎲", "🎯", "🎵", "🎁", "💎", "🔔", "⚽", "🏀"
      ];
      const boardEl = document.getElementById("board");
      const boardShell = document.getElementById("boardShell");
      const pathLayer = document.getElementById("pathLayer");
      const timeEl = document.getElementById("time");
      const movesEl = document.getElementById("moves");
      const pairsEl = document.getElementById("pairs");
      const shufflesEl = document.getElementById("shuffles");
      const statusEl = document.getElementById("status");
      const restartBtn = document.getElementById("restartBtn");
      const shuffleBtn = document.getElementById("shuffleBtn");
      const hintBtn = document.getElementById("hintBtn");
      const difficultyEl = document.getElementById("difficulty");
      const winModal = document.getElementById("winModal");
      const winSummary = document.getElementById("winSummary");
      const playAgainBtn = document.getElementById("playAgainBtn");
      const state = {
        rows: 8,
        cols: 10,
        grid: [],
        selected: null,
        moves: 0,
        matchedPairs: 0,
        totalPairs: 0,
        shuffles: 0,
        startedAt: 0,
        elapsedBeforeStart: 0,
        timerId: null,
        locked: false,
        gameOver: false
      };
      function parseDifficulty(value) {
        const [cols, rows] = value.split("x").map(Number);
        return { rows, cols };
      }
      function setStatus(message, type = "") {
        statusEl.textContent = message;
        statusEl.className = `status ${type}`.trim();
      }
      function formatTime(ms) {
        const totalSeconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
        const minutes = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        const seconds = (totalSeconds % 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        return `${minutes}:${seconds}`;
      }
      function startTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.startedAt = Date.now();
        state.timerId = setInterval(() => {
          timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
        }, 250);
      }
      function stopTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.timerId = null;
      }
      function shuffleArray(array) {
        const copy = [...array];
        for (let i = copy.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
          [copy[i], copy[j]] = [copy[j], copy[i]];
        }
        return copy;
      }
      function buildSolvableValues(rows, cols) {
        const totalCells = rows * cols;
        const totalPairs = Math.floor(totalCells / 2);
        const values = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < totalPairs; i++) {
          const icon = ICONS[i % ICONS.length];
          values.push(icon, icon);
        }
        return shuffleArray(values);
      }
      function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;
        state.locked = false;
        state.gameOver = false;
        winModal.classList.remove("open");
        const values = buildSolvableValues(state.rows, state.cols);
        let index = 0;
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          const row = [];
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateColumns = `repeat(${state.cols}, var(--cell-size))`;
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateRows = `repeat(${state.rows}, var(--cell-size))`;
        renderBoard();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Pick two matching icons to clear them.");
        clearPath();
        startTimer();
        // Avoid rare no-move starting boards by reshuffling live tiles.
        ensureAvailableMove();
      }
      function updateStats() {
        movesEl.textContent = state.moves;
        pairsEl.textContent = `${state.matchedPairs}/${state.totalPairs}`;
        shufflesEl.textContent = state.shuffles;
        timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
      }
      function renderBoard() {
        const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
        boardEl.innerHTML = "";
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            const cell = state.grid[r][c];
            const tile = document.createElement("button");
            tile.type = "button";
            tile.className = `tile${cell.matched ? " empty" : ""}`;
            tile.dataset.row = r;
            tile.dataset.col = c;
            tile.setAttribute("role", "gridcell");
            tile.setAttribute("aria-label", cell.matched ? "empty" : `tile ${cell.value}`);
            tile.textContent = cell.matched ? "" : cell.value;
            tile.addEventListener("click", () => handleTileClick(r, c));
            fragment.appendChild(tile);
          }
        }
        boardEl.appendChild(fragment);
        syncSelectionClass();
      }
      function getTileElement(pos) {
        if (!pos) return null;
        return boardEl.querySelector(`.tile[data-row="${pos.r}"][data-col="${pos.c}"]`);
      }
      function syncSelectionClass() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.selected").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("selected"));
        if (state.selected) {
          const selectedEl = getTileElement(state.selected);
          if (selectedEl) selectedEl.classList.add("selected");
        }
      }
      function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const clicked = { r, c };
        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }
        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }
        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;
        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);
        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");
        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();
          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }
      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }
      function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }
      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }
      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;
        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;
        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];
        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        return result;
      }
      function turnsInPath(points) {
        let turns = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
          const prev = points[i - 1];
          const current = points[i];
          const next = points[i + 1];
          const dir1 = { r: Math.sign(current.r - prev.r), c: Math.sign(current.c - prev.c) };
          const dir2 = { r: Math.sign(next.r - current.r), c: Math.sign(next.c - current.c) };
          if (dir1.r !== dir2.r || dir1.c !== dir2.c) turns++;
        }
        return turns;
      }
      function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;
        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };
        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];
        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;
        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;
          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });
        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();
          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }
          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;
            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };
            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;
            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;
            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }
        return null;
      }
      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");
        const paddingTop = parseFloat(style.paddingTop || "0");
        const step = tileSize + gap;
        return {
          x: boardRect.left - shellRect.left + paddingLeft + point.c * step + tileSize / 2,
          y: boardRect.top - shellRect.top + paddingTop + point.r * step + tileSize / 2
        };
      }
      function drawPath(path) {
        clearPath();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        pathLayer.setAttribute("width", shellRect.width);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("height", shellRect.height);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("viewBox", `0 0 ${shellRect.width} ${shellRect.height}`);
        const points = path.map(cellCenter);
        const polyline = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "polyline");
        polyline.setAttribute("class", "path-line");
        polyline.setAttribute("points", points.map(p => `${p.x},${p.y}`).join(" "));
        pathLayer.appendChild(polyline);
      }
      function clearPath() {
        pathLayer.innerHTML = "";
      }
      function liveTiles() {
        const tiles = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              tiles.push({ r, c, value: state.grid[r][c].value });
            }
          }
        }
        return tiles;
      }
      function findAvailableMove() {
        const byValue = new Map();
        for (const tile of liveTiles()) {
          if (!byValue.has(tile.value)) byValue.set(tile.value, []);
          const group = byValue.get(tile.value);
          for (const other of group) {
            const start = { r: other.r, c: other.c };
            const end = { r: tile.r, c: tile.c };
            const path = findConnection(start, end);
            if (path) return { start, end, path };
          }
          group.push(tile);
        }
        return null;
      }
      function shuffleRemaining({ countMove = false } = {}) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const positions = [];
        const values = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              positions.push({ r, c });
              values.push(state.grid[r][c].value);
            }
          }
        }
        const shuffled = shuffleArray(values);
        positions.forEach((pos, index) => {
          state.grid[pos.r][pos.c].value = shuffled[index];
        });
        state.selected = null;
        state.shuffles++;
        if (countMove) state.moves++;
        renderBoard();
        clearPath();
        updateStats();
        return findAvailableMove();
      }
      function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;
        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;
        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }
        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");
        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }
      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }
      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }
      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");
        }
      });
      hintBtn.addEventListener("click", showHint);
      difficultyEl.addEventListener("change", newGame);
      playAgainBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
        if (pathLayer.children.length) clearPath();
      });
      newGame();
    })();
  </script>

<body>
  <div class="app">
    <header>
      <div class="title-block">
        <h1>Classic Lianliankan</h1>
        <p>Connect identical tiles with a path using no more than two turns. The route may travel through the open border outside the board, but it cannot cross other tiles.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="controls">
        <button id="restartBtn" type="button">Restart</button>
        <button id="shuffleBtn" class="secondary" type="button">Shuffle</button>
        <button id="hintBtn" class="ghost" type="button">Hint</button>
      </div>
    </header>
    <main>
      <section class="board-wrap" aria-label="Lianliankan game board">
        <div id="boardShell" class="board-shell">
          <svg id="pathLayer" class="path-layer" aria-hidden="true"></svg>
          <div id="board" class="board" role="grid" aria-label="Tile grid"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <aside class="sidebar">
        <div class="stats">
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Time</span>
            <span id="time" class="value">00:00</span>

          </div>
          <div class="stat">

            <span id="pairs" class="value">0/40</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">

            <span id="shuffles" class="value">0</span>
          </div>

        <label class="difficulty">
          Board size
          <select id="difficulty">
            <option value="8x6">8 × 6 relaxed</option>

        <div id="status" class="status">Pick two matching icons to clear them.</div>
        <ol class="rules">

          <li>The connection path needs 0, 1, or 2 turns.</li>
          <li>Empty cells and the outside border are open paths.</li>

  <script>
    (() => {
      "use strict";
      const ICONS = [
        "🍎", "🍋", "🍇", "🍓", "🍒", "🍑", "🥝", "🍍", "🥥", "🥑",
        "🐶", "🐱", "🐼", "🦊", "🐸", "🐵", "🐧", "🦄", "🐙", "🦋",
        "⭐", "🌙", "☀️", "🌈", "⚡", "🔥", "❄️", "🌻", "🍄", "🌵",
        "🚗", "🚀", "🎲", "🎯", "🎵", "🎁", "💎", "🔔", "⚽", "🏀"
      ];
      const boardEl = document.getElementById("board");
      const boardShell = document.getElementById("boardShell");
      const pathLayer = document.getElementById("pathLayer");
      const timeEl = document.getElementById("time");
      const movesEl = document.getElementById("moves");
      const pairsEl = document.getElementById("pairs");
      const shufflesEl = document.getElementById("shuffles");
      const statusEl = document.getElementById("status");
      const restartBtn = document.getElementById("restartBtn");
      const shuffleBtn = document.getElementById("shuffleBtn");
      const hintBtn = document.getElementById("hintBtn");
      const difficultyEl = document.getElementById("difficulty");
      const winModal = document.getElementById("winModal");
      const winSummary = document.getElementById("winSummary");
      const playAgainBtn = document.getElementById("playAgainBtn");
      const state = {
        rows: 8,
        cols: 10,
        grid: [],
        selected: null,
        moves: 0,
        matchedPairs: 0,
        totalPairs: 0,
        shuffles: 0,
        startedAt: 0,
        elapsedBeforeStart: 0,
        timerId: null,
        locked: false,
        gameOver: false
      };
      function parseDifficulty(value) {
        const [cols, rows] = value.split("x").map(Number);
        return { rows, cols };
      }
      function setStatus(message, type = "") {
        statusEl.textContent = message;
        statusEl.className = `status ${type}`.trim();
      }
      function formatTime(ms) {
        const totalSeconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
        const minutes = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        const seconds = (totalSeconds % 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        return `${minutes}:${seconds}`;
      }
      function startTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.startedAt = Date.now();
        state.timerId = setInterval(() => {
          timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
        }, 250);
      }
      function stopTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.timerId = null;
      }
      function shuffleArray(array) {
        const copy = [...array];
        for (let i = copy.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
          [copy[i], copy[j]] = [copy[j], copy[i]];
        }
        return copy;
      }
      function buildSolvableValues(rows, cols) {
        const totalCells = rows * cols;
        const totalPairs = Math.floor(totalCells / 2);
        const values = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < totalPairs; i++) {
          const icon = ICONS[i % ICONS.length];
          values.push(icon, icon);
        }
        return shuffleArray(values);
      }
      function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;
        state.locked = false;
        state.gameOver = false;
        winModal.classList.remove("open");
        const values = buildSolvableValues(state.rows, state.cols);
        let index = 0;
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          const row = [];
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateColumns = `repeat(${state.cols}, var(--cell-size))`;
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateRows = `repeat(${state.rows}, var(--cell-size))`;
        renderBoard();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Pick two matching icons to clear them.");
        clearPath();
        startTimer();
        // Avoid rare no-move starting boards by reshuffling live tiles.
        ensureAvailableMove();
      }
      function updateStats() {
        movesEl.textContent = state.moves;
        pairsEl.textContent = `${state.matchedPairs}/${state.totalPairs}`;
        shufflesEl.textContent = state.shuffles;
        timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
      }
      function renderBoard() {
        const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
        boardEl.innerHTML = "";
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            const cell = state.grid[r][c];
            const tile = document.createElement("button");
            tile.type = "button";
            tile.className = `tile${cell.matched ? " empty" : ""}`;
            tile.dataset.row = r;
            tile.dataset.col = c;
            tile.setAttribute("role", "gridcell");
            tile.setAttribute("aria-label", cell.matched ? "empty" : `tile ${cell.value}`);
            tile.textContent = cell.matched ? "" : cell.value;
            tile.addEventListener("click", () => handleTileClick(r, c));
            fragment.appendChild(tile);
          }
        }
        boardEl.appendChild(fragment);
        syncSelectionClass();
      }
      function getTileElement(pos) {
        if (!pos) return null;
        return boardEl.querySelector(`.tile[data-row="${pos.r}"][data-col="${pos.c}"]`);
      }
      function syncSelectionClass() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.selected").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("selected"));
        if (state.selected) {
          const selectedEl = getTileElement(state.selected);
          if (selectedEl) selectedEl.classList.add("selected");
        }
      }
      function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const clicked = { r, c };
        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }
        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }
        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;
        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);
        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");
        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();
          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }
      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }
      function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }
      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }
      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;
        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;
        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];
        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        return result;
      }
      function turnsInPath(points) {
        let turns = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
          const prev = points[i - 1];
          const current = points[i];
          const next = points[i + 1];
          const dir1 = { r: Math.sign(current.r - prev.r), c: Math.sign(current.c - prev.c) };
          const dir2 = { r: Math.sign(next.r - current.r), c: Math.sign(next.c - current.c) };
          if (dir1.r !== dir2.r || dir1.c !== dir2.c) turns++;
        }
        return turns;
      }
      function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;
        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };
        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];
        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;
        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;
          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });
        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();
          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }
          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;
            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };
            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;
            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;
            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }
        return null;
      }
      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");
        const paddingTop = parseFloat(style.paddingTop || "0");
        const step = tileSize + gap;
        return {
          x: boardRect.left - shellRect.left + paddingLeft + point.c * step + tileSize / 2,
          y: boardRect.top - shellRect.top + paddingTop + point.r * step + tileSize / 2
        };
      }
      function drawPath(path) {
        clearPath();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        pathLayer.setAttribute("width", shellRect.width);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("height", shellRect.height);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("viewBox", `0 0 ${shellRect.width} ${shellRect.height}`);
        const points = path.map(cellCenter);
        const polyline = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "polyline");
        polyline.setAttribute("class", "path-line");
        polyline.setAttribute("points", points.map(p => `${p.x},${p.y}`).join(" "));
        pathLayer.appendChild(polyline);
      }
      function clearPath() {
        pathLayer.innerHTML = "";
      }
      function liveTiles() {
        const tiles = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              tiles.push({ r, c, value: state.grid[r][c].value });
            }
          }
        }
        return tiles;
      }
      function findAvailableMove() {
        const byValue = new Map();
        for (const tile of liveTiles()) {
          if (!byValue.has(tile.value)) byValue.set(tile.value, []);
          const group = byValue.get(tile.value);
          for (const other of group) {
            const start = { r: other.r, c: other.c };
            const end = { r: tile.r, c: tile.c };
            const path = findConnection(start, end);
            if (path) return { start, end, path };
          }
          group.push(tile);
        }
        return null;
      }
      function shuffleRemaining({ countMove = false } = {}) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const positions = [];
        const values = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              positions.push({ r, c });
              values.push(state.grid[r][c].value);
            }
          }
        }
        const shuffled = shuffleArray(values);
        positions.forEach((pos, index) => {
          state.grid[pos.r][pos.c].value = shuffled[index];
        });
        state.selected = null;
        state.shuffles++;
        if (countMove) state.moves++;
        renderBoard();
        clearPath();
        updateStats();
        return findAvailableMove();
      }
      function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;
        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;
        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }
        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");
        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }
      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }
      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }
      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");
        }
      });
      hintBtn.addEventListener("click", showHint);
      difficultyEl.addEventListener("change", newGame);
      playAgainBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
        if (pathLayer.children.length) clearPath();
      });
      newGame();
    })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
]]></write_file>
  </actions>
</response>

      display: grid;
      grid-template-columns: 1fr minmax(220px, 280px);
      gap: 16px;
      align-items: start;
    }
    .board-wrap,
    .sidebar {
      border: 1px solid var(--panel-strong);
      border-radius: 24px;
      background: linear-gradient(145deg, rgba(255,255,255,0.14), rgba(255,255,255,0.07));
      box-shadow: 0 18px 48px var(--shadow);
      backdrop-filter: blur(16px);
    }
    .board-wrap {
      position: relative;
      padding: clamp(12px, 2.2vw, 22px);
      overflow: auto;
      min-height: 360px;
    }
    .board-shell {
      position: relative;
      width: max-content;

    }
    .board {
      display: grid;
      grid-template-columns: repeat(10, var(--cell-size));
      grid-template-rows: repeat(8, var(--cell-size));
      gap: var(--gap);
      padding: var(--gap);
      border-radius: 18px;
      background: rgba(8, 18, 34, 0.28);
      box-shadow: inset 0 0 0 1px rgba(255,255,255,0.08);
      touch-action: manipulation;
    }
    .tile {
      width: var(--cell-size);
      height: var(--cell-size);
      display: grid;
      place-items: center;
      border-radius: 15px;
      border: 2px solid var(--tile-border);
      background:
        linear-gradient(145deg, rgba(255,255,255,0.98), rgba(220,235,255,0.88));
      color: #152036;
      font-size: calc(var(--cell-size) * 0.52);
      cursor: pointer;
      user-select: none;
      box-shadow: 0 8px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.18);
      transition:
        opacity 0.2s ease,
        transform 0.14s ease,
        background 0.14s ease,
        border-color 0.14s ease,
        box-shadow 0.14s ease;
    }
    .tile:not(.empty):hover {
      transform: translateY(-2px);
      background: var(--tile-hover);
      box-shadow: 0 12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.24);
    }
    .tile.selected {
      background: linear-gradient(145deg, #fff9cf, var(--tile-selected));
      border-color: var(--warn);
      transform: translateY(-2px) scale(1.04);
      box-shadow: 0 0 0 4px rgba(255, 209, 102, 0.2), 0 14px 26px rgba(0,0,0,0.26);
    }
    .tile.hint {
      animation: hintPulse 0.9s ease-in-out 2;
    }
    .tile.empty {
      opacity: 0;
      pointer-events: none;
      transform: scale(0.64);
    }
    .tile.removing {
      animation: popOut 0.24s ease forwards;
    }
    .path-layer {
      position: absolute;
      inset: 0;
      width: 100%;
      height: 100%;
      overflow: visible;
      pointer-events: none;
    }
    .path-line {
      fill: none;
      stroke: var(--accent);
      stroke-width: 5;

      stroke-linejoin: round;

      stroke-dasharray: 9 8;
      animation: dash 0.55s linear infinite;
    }
    .sidebar {
      padding: 18px;
      display: grid;
      gap: 14px;
    }
    .stats {
      display: grid;

      border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.13);
    }
    .stat .label {
      display: block;
      color: var(--muted);
      font-size: 0.78rem;
      text-transform: uppercase;
      letter-spacing: 0.08em;

    }
    .stat .value {
      font-weight: 900;
      font-size: 1.22rem;
    }
    .status {
      min-height: 54px;

      line-height: 1.42;
    }

      color: var(--accent);
    }

<body>
  <div class="app">
    <header>
      <div class="title-block">
        <h1>Classic Lianliankan</h1>
        <p>Connect identical tiles with a path using no more than two turns. The route may travel through the open border outside the board, but it cannot cross other tiles.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="controls">
        <button id="restartBtn" type="button">Restart</button>
        <button id="shuffleBtn" class="secondary" type="button">Shuffle</button>
        <button id="hintBtn" class="ghost" type="button">Hint</button>
      </div>
    </header>
    <main>
      <section class="board-wrap" aria-label="Lianliankan game board">
        <div id="boardShell" class="board-shell">
          <svg id="pathLayer" class="path-layer" aria-hidden="true"></svg>
          <div id="board" class="board" role="grid" aria-label="Tile grid"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <aside class="sidebar">
        <div class="stats">
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Time</span>
            <span id="time" class="value">00:00</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Moves</span>
            <span id="moves" class="value">0</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Pairs</span>
            <span id="pairs" class="value">0/40</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Shuffles</span>
            <span id="shuffles" class="value">0</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <label class="difficulty">
          Board size
          <select id="difficulty">
            <option value="8x6">8 × 6 relaxed</option>
            <option value="10x8" selected>10 × 8 classic</option>
            <option value="12x8">12 × 8 wide</option>
          </select>
        </label>
        <div id="status" class="status">Pick two matching icons to clear them.</div>
        <ol class="rules">
          <li>Only identical icons can be matched.</li>
          <li>The connection path needs 0, 1, or 2 turns.</li>
          <li>Empty cells and the outside border are open paths.</li>
          <li>Clear all pairs to win.</li>
        </ol>
      </aside>
    </main>
  </div>
  <div id="winModal" class="modal" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="winTitle">
    <div class="dialog">
      <h2 id="winTitle">You cleared the board!</h2>
      <p id="winSummary">Great run.</p>
      <button id="playAgainBtn" type="button">Play Again</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  <script>
    (() => {
      "use strict";
      const ICONS = [
        "🍎", "🍋", "🍇", "🍓", "🍒", "🍑", "🥝", "🍍", "🥥", "🥑",
        "🐶", "🐱", "🐼", "🦊", "🐸", "🐵", "🐧", "🦄", "🐙", "🦋",
        "⭐", "🌙", "☀️", "🌈", "⚡", "🔥", "❄️", "🌻", "🍄", "🌵",
        "🚗", "🚀", "🎲", "🎯", "🎵", "🎁", "💎", "🔔", "⚽", "🏀"
      ];
      const boardEl = document.getElementById("board");
      const boardShell = document.getElementById("boardShell");
      const pathLayer = document.getElementById("pathLayer");
      const timeEl = document.getElementById("time");
      const movesEl = document.getElementById("moves");
      const pairsEl = document.getElementById("pairs");
      const shufflesEl = document.getElementById("shuffles");
      const statusEl = document.getElementById("status");
      const restartBtn = document.getElementById("restartBtn");
      const shuffleBtn = document.getElementById("shuffleBtn");
      const hintBtn = document.getElementById("hintBtn");
      const difficultyEl = document.getElementById("difficulty");
      const winModal = document.getElementById("winModal");
      const winSummary = document.getElementById("winSummary");
      const playAgainBtn = document.getElementById("playAgainBtn");
      const state = {
        rows: 8,
        cols: 10,
        grid: [],
        selected: null,
        moves: 0,
        matchedPairs: 0,
        totalPairs: 0,
        shuffles: 0,
        startedAt: 0,
        elapsedBeforeStart: 0,
        timerId: null,
        locked: false,
        gameOver: false
      };
      function parseDifficulty(value) {
        const [cols, rows] = value.split("x").map(Number);
        return { rows, cols };
      }
      function setStatus(message, type = "") {
        statusEl.textContent = message;
        statusEl.className = `status ${type}`.trim();
      }
      function formatTime(ms) {
        const totalSeconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
        const minutes = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        const seconds = (totalSeconds % 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        return `${minutes}:${seconds}`;
      }
      function startTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.startedAt = Date.now();
        state.timerId = setInterval(() => {
          timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
        }, 250);
      }
      function stopTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.timerId = null;
      }
      function shuffleArray(array) {
        const copy = [...array];
        for (let i = copy.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
          [copy[i], copy[j]] = [copy[j], copy[i]];
        }
        return copy;
      }
      function buildSolvableValues(rows, cols) {
        const totalCells = rows * cols;
        const totalPairs = Math.floor(totalCells / 2);
        const values = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < totalPairs; i++) {
          const icon = ICONS[i % ICONS.length];
          values.push(icon, icon);
        }
        return shuffleArray(values);
      }
      function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;
        state.locked = false;
        state.gameOver = false;
        winModal.classList.remove("open");
        const values = buildSolvableValues(state.rows, state.cols);
        let index = 0;
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          const row = [];
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateColumns = `repeat(${state.cols}, var(--cell-size))`;
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateRows = `repeat(${state.rows}, var(--cell-size))`;
        renderBoard();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Pick two matching icons to clear them.");
        clearPath();
        startTimer();
        // Avoid rare no-move starting boards by reshuffling live tiles.
        ensureAvailableMove();
      }
      function updateStats() {
        movesEl.textContent = state.moves;
        pairsEl.textContent = `${state.matchedPairs}/${state.totalPairs}`;
        shufflesEl.textContent = state.shuffles;
        timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
      }
      function renderBoard() {
        const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
        boardEl.innerHTML = "";
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            const cell = state.grid[r][c];
            const tile = document.createElement("button");
            tile.type = "button";
            tile.className = `tile${cell.matched ? " empty" : ""}`;
            tile.dataset.row = r;
            tile.dataset.col = c;
            tile.setAttribute("role", "gridcell");
            tile.setAttribute("aria-label", cell.matched ? "empty" : `tile ${cell.value}`);
            tile.textContent = cell.matched ? "" : cell.value;
            tile.addEventListener("click", () => handleTileClick(r, c));
            fragment.appendChild(tile);
          }
        }
        boardEl.appendChild(fragment);
        syncSelectionClass();
      }
      function getTileElement(pos) {
        if (!pos) return null;
        return boardEl.querySelector(`.tile[data-row="${pos.r}"][data-col="${pos.c}"]`);
      }
      function syncSelectionClass() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.selected").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("selected"));
        if (state.selected) {
          const selectedEl = getTileElement(state.selected);
          if (selectedEl) selectedEl.classList.add("selected");
        }
      }
      function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const clicked = { r, c };
        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }
        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }
        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;
        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);
        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");
        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();
          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }
      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }
      function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }
      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }
      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;
        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;
        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];
        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        return result;
      }
      function turnsInPath(points) {
        let turns = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
          const prev = points[i - 1];
          const current = points[i];
          const next = points[i + 1];
          const dir1 = { r: Math.sign(current.r - prev.r), c: Math.sign(current.c - prev.c) };
          const dir2 = { r: Math.sign(next.r - current.r), c: Math.sign(next.c - current.c) };
          if (dir1.r !== dir2.r || dir1.c !== dir2.c) turns++;
        }
        return turns;
      }
      function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;
        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };
        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];
        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;
        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;
          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });
        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();
          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }
          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;
            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };
            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;
            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;
            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }
        return null;
      }
      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");
        const paddingTop = parseFloat(style.paddingTop || "0");
        const step = tileSize + gap;
        return {
          x: boardRect.left - shellRect.left + paddingLeft + point.c * step + tileSize / 2,
          y: boardRect.top - shellRect.top + paddingTop + point.r * step + tileSize / 2
        };
      }
      function drawPath(path) {
        clearPath();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        pathLayer.setAttribute("width", shellRect.width);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("height", shellRect.height);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("viewBox", `0 0 ${shellRect.width} ${shellRect.height}`);
        const points = path.map(cellCenter);
        const polyline = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "polyline");
        polyline.setAttribute("class", "path-line");
        polyline.setAttribute("points", points.map(p => `${p.x},${p.y}`).join(" "));
        pathLayer.appendChild(polyline);
      }
      function clearPath() {
        pathLayer.innerHTML = "";
      }
      function liveTiles() {
        const tiles = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              tiles.push({ r, c, value: state.grid[r][c].value });
            }
          }
        }
        return tiles;
      }
      function findAvailableMove() {
        const byValue = new Map();
        for (const tile of liveTiles()) {
          if (!byValue.has(tile.value)) byValue.set(tile.value, []);
          const group = byValue.get(tile.value);
          for (const other of group) {
            const start = { r: other.r, c: other.c };
            const end = { r: tile.r, c: tile.c };
            const path = findConnection(start, end);
            if (path) return { start, end, path };
          }
          group.push(tile);
        }
        return null;
      }
      function shuffleRemaining({ countMove = false } = {}) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const positions = [];
        const values = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              positions.push({ r, c });
              values.push(state.grid[r][c].value);
            }
          }
        }
        const shuffled = shuffleArray(values);
        positions.forEach((pos, index) => {
          state.grid[pos.r][pos.c].value = shuffled[index];
        });
        state.selected = null;
        state.shuffles++;
        if (countMove) state.moves++;
        renderBoard();
        clearPath();
        updateStats();
        return findAvailableMove();
      }
      function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;
        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;
        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }
        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");
        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }
      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }
      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }
      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");
        }
      });
      hintBtn.addEventListener("click", showHint);
      difficultyEl.addEventListener("change", newGame);
      playAgainBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
        if (pathLayer.children.length) clearPath();
      });
      newGame();
    })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
]]></write_file>
  </actions>
</response>

<body>
  <div class="app">
    <header>
      <div class="title-block">
        <h1>Classic Lianliankan</h1>
        <p>Connect identical tiles with a path using no more than two turns. The route may travel through the open border outside the board, but it cannot cross other tiles.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="controls">
        <button id="restartBtn" type="button">Restart</button>
        <button id="shuffleBtn" class="secondary" type="button">Shuffle</button>
        <button id="hintBtn" class="ghost" type="button">Hint</button>
      </div>
    </header>
    <main>
      <section class="board-wrap" aria-label="Lianliankan game board">
        <div id="boardShell" class="board-shell">
          <svg id="pathLayer" class="path-layer" aria-hidden="true"></svg>
          <div id="board" class="board" role="grid" aria-label="Tile grid"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <aside class="sidebar">
        <div class="stats">
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Time</span>
            <span id="time" class="value">00:00</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Moves</span>
            <span id="moves" class="value">0</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Pairs</span>
            <span id="pairs" class="value">0/40</span>
          </div>
          <div class="stat">
            <span class="label">Shuffles</span>
            <span id="shuffles" class="value">0</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <label class="difficulty">
          Board size
          <select id="difficulty">
            <option value="8x6">8 × 6 relaxed</option>

  <div id="winModal" class="modal" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="winTitle">
    <div class="dialog">
