  <script>
    (() => {
      "use strict";
      const ICONS = [
        "🍎", "🍋", "🍇", "🍓", "🍒", "🍑", "🥝", "🍍", "🥥", "🥑",
        "🐶", "🐱", "🐼", "🦊", "🐸", "🐵", "🐧", "🦄", "🐙", "🦋",
        "⭐", "🌙", "☀️", "🌈", "⚡", "🔥", "❄️", "🌻", "🍄", "🌵",
        "🚗", "🚀", "🎲", "🎯", "🎵", "🎁", "💎", "🔔", "⚽", "🏀"
      ];
      const boardEl = document.getElementById("board");
      const boardShell = document.getElementById("boardShell");
      const pathLayer = document.getElementById("pathLayer");
      const timeEl = document.getElementById("time");
      const movesEl = document.getElementById("moves");
      const pairsEl = document.getElementById("pairs");
      const shufflesEl = document.getElementById("shuffles");
      const statusEl = document.getElementById("status");
      const restartBtn = document.getElementById("restartBtn");
      const shuffleBtn = document.getElementById("shuffleBtn");
      const hintBtn = document.getElementById("hintBtn");
      const difficultyEl = document.getElementById("difficulty");
      const winModal = document.getElementById("winModal");
      const winSummary = document.getElementById("winSummary");
      const playAgainBtn = document.getElementById("playAgainBtn");
      const state = {
        rows: 8,
        cols: 10,
        grid: [],
        selected: null,
        moves: 0,
        matchedPairs: 0,
        totalPairs: 0,
        shuffles: 0,
        startedAt: 0,
        elapsedBeforeStart: 0,
        timerId: null,
        locked: false,
        gameOver: false
      };
      function parseDifficulty(value) {
        const [cols, rows] = value.split("x").map(Number);
        return { rows, cols };
      }
      function setStatus(message, type = "") {
        statusEl.textContent = message;
        statusEl.className = `status ${type}`.trim();
      }
      function formatTime(ms) {
        const totalSeconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
        const minutes = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        const seconds = (totalSeconds % 60).toString().padStart(2, "0");
        return `${minutes}:${seconds}`;
      }
      function startTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.startedAt = Date.now();
        state.timerId = setInterval(() => {
          timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
        }, 250);
      }
      function stopTimer() {
        clearInterval(state.timerId);
        state.timerId = null;
      }
      function shuffleArray(array) {
        const copy = [...array];
        for (let i = copy.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
          [copy[i], copy[j]] = [copy[j], copy[i]];
        }
        return copy;
      }
      function buildSolvableValues(rows, cols) {
        const totalCells = rows * cols;
        const totalPairs = Math.floor(totalCells / 2);
        const values = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < totalPairs; i++) {
          const icon = ICONS[i % ICONS.length];
          values.push(icon, icon);
        }
        return shuffleArray(values);
      }
      function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;
        state.locked = false;
        state.gameOver = false;
        winModal.classList.remove("open");
        const values = buildSolvableValues(state.rows, state.cols);
        let index = 0;
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          const row = [];
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateColumns = `repeat(${state.cols}, var(--cell-size))`;
        boardEl.style.gridTemplateRows = `repeat(${state.rows}, var(--cell-size))`;
        renderBoard();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Pick two matching icons to clear them.");
        clearPath();
        startTimer();
        // Avoid rare no-move starting boards by reshuffling live tiles.
        ensureAvailableMove();
      }
      function updateStats() {
        movesEl.textContent = state.moves;
        pairsEl.textContent = `${state.matchedPairs}/${state.totalPairs}`;
        shufflesEl.textContent = state.shuffles;
        timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);
      }
      function renderBoard() {
        const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
        boardEl.innerHTML = "";
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            const cell = state.grid[r][c];
            const tile = document.createElement("button");
            tile.type = "button";
            tile.className = `tile${cell.matched ? " empty" : ""}`;
            tile.dataset.row = r;
            tile.dataset.col = c;
            tile.setAttribute("role", "gridcell");
            tile.setAttribute("aria-label", cell.matched ? "empty" : `tile ${cell.value}`);
            tile.textContent = cell.matched ? "" : cell.value;
            tile.addEventListener("click", () => handleTileClick(r, c));
            fragment.appendChild(tile);
          }
        }
        boardEl.appendChild(fragment);
        syncSelectionClass();
      }
      function getTileElement(pos) {
        if (!pos) return null;
        return boardEl.querySelector(`.tile[data-row="${pos.r}"][data-col="${pos.c}"]`);
      }
      function syncSelectionClass() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.selected").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("selected"));
        if (state.selected) {
          const selectedEl = getTileElement(state.selected);
          if (selectedEl) selectedEl.classList.add("selected");
        }
      }
      function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const clicked = { r, c };
        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }
        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }
        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;
        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }
        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);
        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");
        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();
          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }
      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }
      function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }
      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }
      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;
        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;
        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];
        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        return result;
      }
      function turnsInPath(points) {
        let turns = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
          const prev = points[i - 1];
          const current = points[i];
          const next = points[i + 1];
          const dir1 = { r: Math.sign(current.r - prev.r), c: Math.sign(current.c - prev.c) };
          const dir2 = { r: Math.sign(next.r - current.r), c: Math.sign(next.c - current.c) };
          if (dir1.r !== dir2.r || dir1.c !== dir2.c) turns++;
        }
        return turns;
      }
      function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;
        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };
        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];
        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;
        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;
          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });
        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();
          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }
          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;
            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };
            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;
            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;
            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }
        return null;
      }
      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");
        const paddingTop = parseFloat(style.paddingTop || "0");
        const step = tileSize + gap;
        return {
          x: boardRect.left - shellRect.left + paddingLeft + point.c * step + tileSize / 2,
          y: boardRect.top - shellRect.top + paddingTop + point.r * step + tileSize / 2
        };
      }
      function drawPath(path) {
        clearPath();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        pathLayer.setAttribute("width", shellRect.width);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("height", shellRect.height);
        pathLayer.setAttribute("viewBox", `0 0 ${shellRect.width} ${shellRect.height}`);
        const points = path.map(cellCenter);
        const polyline = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "polyline");
        polyline.setAttribute("class", "path-line");
        polyline.setAttribute("points", points.map(p => `${p.x},${p.y}`).join(" "));
        pathLayer.appendChild(polyline);
      }
      function clearPath() {
        pathLayer.innerHTML = "";
      }
      function liveTiles() {
        const tiles = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              tiles.push({ r, c, value: state.grid[r][c].value });
            }
          }
        }
        return tiles;
      }
      function findAvailableMove() {
        const byValue = new Map();
        for (const tile of liveTiles()) {
          if (!byValue.has(tile.value)) byValue.set(tile.value, []);
          const group = byValue.get(tile.value);
          for (const other of group) {
            const start = { r: other.r, c: other.c };
            const end = { r: tile.r, c: tile.c };
            const path = findConnection(start, end);
            if (path) return { start, end, path };
          }
          group.push(tile);
        }
        return null;
      }
      function shuffleRemaining({ countMove = false } = {}) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        const positions = [];
        const values = [];
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            if (!state.grid[r][c].matched) {
              positions.push({ r, c });
              values.push(state.grid[r][c].value);
            }
          }
        }
        const shuffled = shuffleArray(values);
        positions.forEach((pos, index) => {
          state.grid[pos.r][pos.c].value = shuffled[index];
        });
        state.selected = null;
        state.shuffles++;
        if (countMove) state.moves++;
        renderBoard();
        clearPath();
        updateStats();
        return findAvailableMove();
      }
      function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;
        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;
        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      }
      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();
        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }
        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");
        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }
      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }
      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }
      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");
        }
      });
      hintBtn.addEventListener("click", showHint);
      difficultyEl.addEventListener("change", newGame);
      playAgainBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);
      window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
        if (pathLayer.children.length) clearPath();
      });
      newGame();
    })();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
]]></write_file>

--- function handleTileClick at 6122 ---
function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;

        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;

        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const clicked = { r, c };

        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }

        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }

        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;

        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);

        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");

        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();

          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }

      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }

      f

--- function checkWin at -1 ---

--- function handleTileClick at 6122 ---
function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;

        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;

        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const clicked = { r, c };

        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }

        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }

        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;

        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);

        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");

        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();

          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }

      function samePos(a, b) {
        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;
      }

      f

--- function findConnection at 10202 ---
function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;

        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };

        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];

        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;

        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;

          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });

        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();

          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }

          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;

            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };

            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;

            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;

            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }

        return null;
      }

      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");
        

--- function isStraightClear at -1 ---

--- function isEmptyForPath at -1 ---

--- function ensureAvailableMove at 15547 ---
function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");

        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }

      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }

      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "wi...

function handleTileClick(r, c) {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;

        const cell = state.grid[r][c];
        if (!cell || cell.matched) return;

        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const clicked = { r, c };

        if (!state.selected) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus(`Selected ${cell.value}. Now pick its matching partner.`);
          return;
        }

        if (samePos(state.selected, clicked)) {
          state.selected = null;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Selection cleared.");
          return;
        }

        const first = state.selected;
        const firstCell = state.grid[first.r][first.c];
        state.moves++;

        if (firstCell.value !== cell.value) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Those icons are different. Try matching identical tiles.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        const path = findConnection(first, clicked);
        if (!path) {
          state.selected = clicked;
          syncSelectionClass();
          setStatus("Blocked path: a match needs no more than two turns.", "bad");
          updateStats();
          return;
        }

        state.locked = true;
        state.selected = null;
        syncSelectionClass();
        drawPath(path);

        const firstEl = getTileElement(first);
        const secondEl = getTileElement(clicked);
        firstEl?.classList.add("removing");
        secondEl?.classList.add("removing");

        setTimeout(() => {
          state.grid[first.r][first.c].matched = true;
          state.grid[clicked.r][clicked.c].matched = true;
          state.matchedPairs++;
          state.locked = false;
          renderBoard();
          clearPath();
          updateStats();

          if (state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) {
            winGame();
          } else {
            setStatus("Matched! Keep going.", "good");
            ensureAvailableMove();
          }
        }, 260);
      }

        return a && b && a.r === b.r && a.c === b.c;

--- function findConnection at 10202 ---
function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;

        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };

        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];

        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;

        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;

          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });

        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();

          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }

          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;

            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };

            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;

            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;

            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }

        return null;
      }

      function cellCenter(point) {
        const boardRect = boardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const shellRect = boardShell.getBoundingClientRect();
        const firstTile = boardEl.querySelector(".tile");
        const tileSize = firstTile ? firstTile.getBoundingClientRect().width : 48;
        const style = getComputedStyle(boardEl);
        const gap = parseFloat(style.gap || "0");
        const paddingLeft = parseFloat(style.paddingLeft || "0");

function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();

          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");

        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");

      }

function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;

              matched: false
            });

        const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();

        boardEl.innerHTML = "";

--- function isInside at 8321 ---
function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }

      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }

      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;

        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;

        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];

        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }

        return result;
      }

      function turnsInPath(points) {
        let turns = 0;
        for (let i = 1; i < points.length - 1; i++) {
          const prev = points[i - 1];
          const current = points[i];
          const next = points[i + 1];
          const dir1 = { r: Math.sign(current.r - prev.r), c: Math.sign(current.c - prev.c) };
          const dir2 = { r: Math.sign(next.r - current.r), c: Math.sign(next.c - current.c) };
          if (dir1.r !== dir2

--- function findConnection at 10202 ---
function findConnection(start, end) {
        if (samePos(start, end)) return null;

        const bounds = {
          minR: -1,
          maxR: state.rows,
          minC: -1,
          maxC: state.cols
        };

        const queue = [];
        const visited = new Map();
        const dirs = [
          { r: -1, c: 0 },
          { r: 1, c: 0 },
          { r: 0, c: -1 },
          { r: 0, c: 1 }
        ];

        const key = (p, dirIndex, turns) => `${p.r},${p.c},${dirIndex},${turns}`;

        dirs.forEach((dir, dirIndex) => {
          const next = { r: start.r + dir.r, c: start.c + dir.c };
          if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) return;
          if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) return;

          const item = {
            pos: next,
            dirIndex,
            turns: 0,
            path: [start, next]
          };
          queue.push(item);
          visited.set(key(next, dirIndex, 0), true);
        });

        while (queue.length) {
          const current = queue.shift();

          if (samePos(current.pos, end)) {
            const path = compressPath(current.path);
            return turnsInPath(path) <= 2 ? path : null;
          }

          for (let dirIndex = 0; dirIndex < dirs.length; dirIndex++) {
            const dir = dirs[dirIndex];
            const turns = current.turns + (dirIndex === current.dirIndex ? 0 : 1);
            if (turns > 2) continue;

            const next = {
              r: current.pos.r + dir.r,
              c: current.pos.c + dir.c
            };

            if (next.r < bounds.minR || next.r > bounds.maxR || next.c < bounds.minC || next.c > bounds.maxC) continue;
            if (!isOpen(next, start, end)) continue;

            const visitKey = key(next, dirIndex, turns);
            if (visited.has(visitKey)) continue;

            visited.set(visitKey, true);
            queue.push({
              pos: next,
              dirIndex,
              turns,
              path: [...current.path, next]
            });
          }
        }

        return null;
      }

      function cellCenter(point) {

function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");

        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }

      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }

function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }

      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }

      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;

        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;

        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];

        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }

        return result;
      }

6. When the TODO is not complete, you MUST NOT set `next_behavior`; omitting it lets the behavior proceed to the next Step.

## Completion

- If the TODO is complete, you MUST write a final `<report>`, exec_bash `todo done $summary` to finish the todo as successful, and set `next_behavior = END`.
- If the TODO cannot be completed, you MUST write a final `<report>` with the blocker or failure cause, exec_bash `todo failed $summary` to finish the todo as failed, and set `next_behavior = END`.
- MUST 
- If user input is required, you MUST use action `sendmsg` and set `next_behavior = WAIT_FOR_MSG`.

## Failure Handling

- On the first failure, you MUST identify the cause and either retry with a changed approach or choose an action that reduces uncertainty.
- If the same cause fails twice without new evidence or a new strategy, you MUST stop and report failure.

## Hard Rules

- You MUST NOT present unverified guesses as facts.
- You MUST NOT replay memory or Step Records as a transcript.
- You MUST NOT perform empty process steps; every action MUST reduce the remaining gap.

## Behavior Loop StepRecords:

Behavior Loop history is not a plain chat log. Each round becomes one
StepRecord: the assistant side is the step intent, and the user side is the
system's action results.

Newer current-behavior StepRecords are kept as full StepRounds. Older records
may be compacted, and records inherited from other behaviors are rendered as
history records or summaries. These compressed records preserve meaning, not
complete detail.

Use StepRecords as execution memory:

- Continue from the latest full StepRound.
- Treat compact/history/summary records as background context.
- Do not treat another behavior's old intent as an instruction for the current
  behavior.



<</PROCESS_RULES>>

function isInside(p) {
        return p.r >= 0 && p.r < state.rows && p.c >= 0 && p.c < state.cols;
      }

      function isOpen(p, start, end) {
        if (!isInside(p)) return true;
        if (samePos(p, start) || samePos(p, end)) return true;
        return state.grid[p.r][p.c].matched;
      }

      function clearStraight(a, b, start, end) {
        if (a.r !== b.r && a.c !== b.c) return false;

        const dr = Math.sign(b.r - a.r);
        const dc = Math.sign(b.c - a.c);
        let r = a.r + dr;
        let c = a.c + dc;

        while (r !== b.r || c !== b.c) {
          if (!isOpen({ r, c }, start, end)) return false;
          r += dr;
          c += dc;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function compressPath(points) {
        const result = [];

        for (const point of points) {
          result.push(point);
          while (result.length >= 3) {
            const a = result[result.length - 3];
            const b = result[result.length - 2];
            const c = result[result.length - 1];
            const sameRow = a.r === b.r && b.r === c.r;
            const sameCol = a.c === b.c && b.c === c.c;
            if (sameRow || sameCol) {
              result.splice(result.length - 2, 1);
            } else {
              break;
            }
          }
        }

        return result;
      }

function turns(path) {
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
    const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
    const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
    const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
    if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
  }
  return n;
}

  context.state.shuffles = 0;
  context.state.grid = values.map(row => row.map(v => v === null ? {value:'·', matched:true} : {value:v, matched:false}));

   - enough information: edit, write, run, or produce the artifact.
   - needs confidence: test, diff, validate, or inspect output.
4. You MUST use the selected skills when they apply.
5. You MAY mix reading, editing, and verification in one step when the action is coherent.
6. When the TODO is not complete, you MUST NOT set `next_behavior`; omitting it lets the behavior proceed to the next Step.

## Completion

- If the TODO is complete, you MUST write a final `<report>`, exec_bash `todo done $summary` to finish the todo as successful, and set `next_behavior = END`.
- If the TODO cannot be completed, you MUST write a final `<report>` with the blocker or failure cause, exec_bash `todo failed $summary` to finish the todo as failed, and set `next_behavior = END`.
- MUST 
- If user input is required, you MUST use action `sendmsg` and set `next_behavior = WAIT_FOR_MSG`.

## Failure Handling

- On the first failure, you MUST identify the cause and either retry with a changed approach or choose an action that reduces uncertainty.
- If the same cause fails twice without new evidence or a new strategy, you MUST stop and report failure.

## Hard Rules

- You MUST NOT present unverified guesses as facts.
- You MUST NOT replay memory or Step Records as a transcript.
- You MUST NOT perform empty process steps; every action MUST reduce the remaining gap.

## Behavior Loop StepRecords:

Behavior Loop history is not a plain chat log. Each round becomes one
StepRecord: the assistant side is the step intent, and the user side is the
system's action results.

Newer current-behavior StepRecords are kept as full StepRounds. Older records
may be compacted, and records inherited from other behaviors are rendered as
history records or summaries. These compressed records preserve meaning, not
complete detail.

Use StepRecords as execution memory:

- Continue from the latest full StepRound.
- Treat compact/history/summary records as background context.
- Do not treat another behavior's old intent as an instruction for the current
  behavior.



<</PROCESS_RULES>>

  ]]></report>

</response>
```

## next_behavior
- MUST set `<next_behavior>` only when `<actions>` is empty; action execution results MUST be observed before changing behavior.
- `<next_behavior>` is the key field used to maintain the behavior state machine and MUST follow the process rules.

## <actions> Usage Rules

- You SHOULD always prefer `write_file` / `edit_file` / `read` over `exec_bash`.
- `<exec_bash>` SHOULD contain bash commands in its body, and each `<exec_bash>` SHOULD complete exactly one task.
- You MUST use `<write_file>` or `<edit_file>` to write text files. You MUST NOT use `echo`, `cat`, or heredoc to write files.

function turns(path) {
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
    const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
    const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
    const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
    if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
  }
  return n;
}

function turns(path) {
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
    const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
    const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
    const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
    if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
  }
  return n;
}
function setGrid(values) {
  game.state.rows = values.length;
  game.state.cols = values[0].length;
  game.state.totalPairs = Math.floor(values.flat().filter(Boolean).length / 2);
  game.state.matchedPairs = 0;
  game.state.shuffles = 0;
  game.state.moves = 0;
  game.state.selected = null;
  game.state.locked = false;
  game.state.gameOver = false;
  game.state.grid = values.map(row => row.map(v => v === null ? {value:'·', matched:true} : {value:v, matched:false}));
}
setGrid([
  ['A','A'],
  ['B','B']
]);

function turns(path) {
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
    const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
    const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
    const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
    if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
  }
  return n;
}
function setGrid(values) {
  game.state.rows = values.length;
  game.state.cols = values[0].length;
  game.state.totalPairs = Math.floor(values.flat().filter(Boolean).length / 2);

  game.state.shuffles = 0;
  game.state.moves = 0;
  game.state.selected = null;

  game.state.gameOver = false;
  game.state.grid = values.map(row => row.map(v => v === null ? {value:'·', matched:true} : {value:v, matched:false}));
}

===== function ensureAvailableMove @ 15547 =====
function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");

        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }

      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }

      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");

function turns(path) {
  let n = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
    const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
    const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
    const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
    if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
  }
  return n;
}

function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;

        const values = buildSolvableValues(state.rows, state.cols);
        let index = 0;
        for (let r = 0; r < state.rows; r++) {
          const row = [];
          for (let c = 0; c < state.cols; c++) {
            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }

===== function ensureAvailableMove @ 15547 =====
function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");

        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }

      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }

      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }

      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);

      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");

function newGame() {
        const size = parseDifficulty(difficultyEl.value);
        state.rows = size.rows;
        state.cols = size.cols;
        state.totalPairs = (state.rows * state.cols) / 2;
        state.grid = [];
        state.selected = null;
        state.moves = 0;
        state.matchedPairs = 0;
        state.shuffles = 0;
        state.elapsedBeforeStart = 0;

        state.gameOver = false;

            row.push({
              value: values[index++],
              matched: false
            });
          }
          state.grid.push(row);
        }

        shufflesEl.textContent = state.shuffles;
        timeEl.textContent = formatTime(Date.now() - state.startedAt + state.elapsedBeforeStart);

===== function ensureAvailableMove @ 15547 =====
function ensureAvailableMove() {
        if (state.gameOver || state.matchedPairs === state.totalPairs) return true;

        let move = findAvailableMove();
        let attempts = 0;

        while (!move && attempts < 20) {
          move = shuffleRemaining();
          attempts++;
        }

        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal moves found after reshuffling. Restart for a fresh board.", "bad");
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      }

      function showHint() {
        if (state.locked || state.gameOver) return;
        clearHint();
        clearPath();

        const move = findAvailableMove();
        if (!move) {
          setStatus("No legal move is available. Try Shuffle.", "bad");
          return;
        }

        const a = getTileElement(move.start);
        const b = getTileElement(move.end);
        a?.classList.add("hint");
        b?.classList.add("hint");
        setStatus("Hint highlighted a connectable pair.", "good");

        setTimeout(clearHint, 1900);
      }

      function clearHint() {
        boardEl.querySelectorAll(".tile.hint").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hint"));
      }

      function winGame() {
        state.gameOver = true;
        stopTimer();
        updateStats();
        setStatus("Victory! You cleared every pair.", "win");
        winSummary.textContent = `Finished in ${timeEl.textContent} with ${state.moves} moves and ${state.shuffles} shuffle${state.shuffles === 1 ? "" : "s"}.`;
        winModal.classList.add("open");
      }

      restartBtn.addEventListener("click", newGame);

      shuffleBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
        shuffleRemaining({ countMove: true });
        if (ensureAvailableMove()) {
          setStatus("Remaining tiles shuffled.", "good");
        }
      });...
[truncated]
```

  function turns(path) {
    let n = 0;
    for (let i = 1; i < path.length - 1; i++) {
      const a = path[i-1], b = path[i], c = path[i+1];
      const d1 = [Math.sign(b.r-a.r), Math.sign(b.c-a.c)];
      const d2 = [Math.sign(c.r-b.r), Math.sign(c.c-b.c)];
      if (d1[0] !== d2[0] || d1[1] !== d2[1]) n++;
    }
    return n;
  }
  function setGrid(vals) {
    game.state.rows = vals.length;
    game.state.cols = vals[0].length;
    game.state.totalPairs = Math.floor(vals.flat().filter(v => v !== null).length / 2);
    game.state.matchedPairs = 0;
    game.state.shuffles = 0;
    game.state.moves = 0;

  }
  console.log('test: direct path');
  setGrid([['A','A'],['B','B']]);
  let p = game.findConnection({r:0,c:0},{r:0,c:1});
  assert(p && turns(p) === 0, 'direct adjacent connection failed');
  console.log('test: one/two-turn through empty cells');
  setGrid([['A','X','A'],[null,null,null],['B','B',null]]);
  p = game.findConnection({r:0,c:0},{r:0,c:2});
  assert(p && turns(p) <= 2, 'blocked row connection through empty cells failed');
  console.log('test: outside border');
  setGrid([['A','X','A'],['X','X','X'],['B','B','X']]);
  p = game.findConnection({r:0,c:0},{r:0,c:2});
  assert(p && turns(p) <= 2 && p.some(pt => pt.r < 0 || pt.c < 0 || pt.r >= game.state.rows || pt.c >= game.state.cols), 'outside border connection failed');
  console.log('test: reject >2 turns');
  setGrid([['A','X','B'],['X','X','X'],['B','X','A']]);
  p = game.findConnection({r:0,c:0},{r:2,c:2});

  console.log('test: selection/removal flow');
  setGrid([['A','A'],['B','B']]);

  game.handleTileClick(0,1);
  assert(game.state.grid[0][0].matched && game.state.grid[0][1].matched, 'matching second click did not remove pair');
  assert(game.state.matchedPairs === 1 && game.state.moves === 1, 'match counters not incremented');
  console.log('test: shuffle behavior');
  setGrid([['A','B'],['A','B']]);

  const move = game.shuffleRemaining();
  const after = game.state.grid.flat().filter(x => !x.matched).map(x => x.value).sort().join('');
  assert(before === after, 'shuffle changed tile multiset');
  assert(game.state.shuffles >= 1, 'shuffle counter not incremented');
  assert(move === false || (move.start && move.end), 'shuffle return shape invalid');
